	}

	}

		conditional_modifier = {
			trigger = {
				owner = {
					mission_completed = unite_the_empire
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				diplomatic_annexation_cost = -0.15
			}
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {	
		owner = {
				add_estate_loyalty = {
    estate = estate_nobles
    loyalty = 20
}
		}
		}
	}
}
